[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A Jazzer fuzzer invocation triggered a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         indicating a file path traversal violation. The error arose during archive          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         expansion in Apache Commons Compress’s `Expander` example code, where the security  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sanitizer detected an attempt to write files outside the intended output directory. [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Issue                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           During fuzz testing with Jazzer, the `FilePathTraversal.check` method raised a    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         critical security issue when expanding archive entries. The sanitizer identified    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         that an extracted file path resolved to `[35m/tmp/[0m…[35m/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`, which [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         did not conform to the allowed extraction directory structure.                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Vulnerability Type                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The issue is classified as a file path traversal vulnerability: malicious archive [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         entries can reference parent directories or otherwise escape the intended           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         extraction root.                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Observations and Findings                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The exception stack trace shows the failure occurs in                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.check` and its helper    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `checkPath` and `copyMismatchMvHook`.                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The `Expander.expand` method in                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples` is where archive entries are       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         processed and written to disk.                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The fuzzer harness entry point is `ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`, which    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         feeds arbitrary data to the `Expander.expand` logic.                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The sanitizer flags attempts to create or move files outside the designated     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         output directory, indicating archive entry names with traversal components [1m([0me.g.,   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         “..[35m/[0m”[1m)[0m or absolute paths.                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Code Areas for Investigation                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. `FilePathTraversal` class [1m([0mlines around check, checkPath, copyMismatchMvHook[1m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         for how paths are validated and normalized.                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. `Expander` example implementation, especially the methods at lines [1;36m216[0m, [1;36m336[0m,   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m412[0m, and [1;36m502[0m, where entries are extracted and written to disk.                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. Interaction between the fuzzer harness [1m([0m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[1m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         and the `Expander` logic to understand how input data is interpreted as archive     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         entries.                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Here is the initial issue log of the codebase:                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m<[0m[1;95missue[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The path traversal arises because the generic `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mArchiveEntrySupplier, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mArchiveEntryBiConsumer, Path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method computes a destination path via [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich itself only does a [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`-and-`[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check on the raw path string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and then [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munconditionally creates directories or writes files there. Malicious entry names [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontaining traversal components or exploiting symlinks can slip through and lead to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrites outside `targetDirectory`, triggering Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Approach  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   We will harden the generic `expand` method by inserting an explicit canonical [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath check immediately after determining each entry’s target path. This check will [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muse absolute, normalized paths to ensure no writes occur outside the intended root,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregardless of archive format. We do not modify any harness, fuzzing logic, or [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `Expander.java`, locate the core generic expand overload [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m94[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private <T extends ArchiveEntry> void [0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              final ArchiveEntrySupplier<T> supplier,[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              final ArchiveEntryBiConsumer<T> writer,[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              final Path targetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          final boolean nullTarget = targetDirectory == null;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m current code:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          final Path targetDirPath = nullTarget ? null : [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtargetDirectory.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[33m...[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Immediately after computing `targetDirPath`, compute its absolute, normalized[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mform once:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          final Path safeBase = nullTarget[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  ? null[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  : [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Inside the extraction loop, replace the single call to `resolveIn` with two [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msteps:  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Resolve the raw entry name against `safeBase`.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Normalize to an absolute path.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Enforce that the resulting path starts with `safeBase`.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Concretely, change:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          final Path targetPath = nullTarget[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  ? null[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  : [0m[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      to:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          final Path targetPath;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnullTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              targetPath = null;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Resolve and normalize[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              Path resolved = [0m[1;35msafeBase.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mnextEntry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                     [0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                     [0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Check against the extraction root[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mresolved.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                      [0m[32m"File path traversal: '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m,[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                      [0m[1;35mnextEntry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, resolved[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              targetPath = resolved;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Delete or bypass the prior `nextEntry.resolveIn` invocation, since we [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanually apply the robust check. Leave the rest of the loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdirectory creation, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile writing[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m unchanged.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Remove the now-unnecessary interface default logic in [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ArchiveEntry.resolveIn` for the example code path, or leave it in place as a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfallback for non-Path-based overloads; our manual check supersedes it for this [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcritical path.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Consistency with the ZIP-specific branch: that code already uses `[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to prevent zip-slip. We apply the same robust pattern across all[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive types.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Simplicity: using `[0m[1;35mtoAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` ensures relative segments [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`..[0m[35m/[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are collapsed and path comparisons are accurate without relying on disk [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexistence [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`toRealPath`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Coverage: this change sits in the single generic extraction loop, covering 7z,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTAR, ZIP and autodetected formats invoked via `ArchiveInputStream`.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preservation of functionality: valid safe paths remain unaffected. Directory [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreation and file writes proceed normally inside the root. Tests and harness remain[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If an entry name legitimately begins with a root-like component but is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended to land inside a subdirectory [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., entries starting `[0m[35m/[0m[95musr[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Those [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentries will now throw IOException. This matches best practice: absolute entry [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnames are unsafe by default.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing tests extracting archives with symlinks inside the root should [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue to work—symlink targets are not followed by this check until after file [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreation, so symlinks within the root are preserved.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If downstream code relied on the old `resolveIn` behavior in rare corner [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcases, those are in the example code only, so risk is minimal.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Reference  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The ZIP branch at lines [0m[1;36m491[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m497[0m[39m in `Expander.java` already uses `[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+ `[0m[1;35m.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for safety. We mirror that pattern here.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Common “zip-slip” mitigation guidance recommends exactly this comparison:  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Path canonicalChild = [0m[1;35mchild.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mcanonicalChild.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcanonicalBase[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Entry is outside target dir"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By consolidating in the generic loop, all archive formats inherit the same [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotection.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. No Harness or Test Changes  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   We do not modify any fuzz harness code or existing tests. The harness will now [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill feed data through the same code path, but malicious inputs will be rejected [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby an IOException before any out-of-bounds writes occur, silencing the fuzzer’s [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity sanitizer.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter applying the patch, rebuild the project and re-run the Jazzer fuzzer to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirm that no `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exceptions arise from path traversal [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A Jazzer coverage-guided fuzzer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m feeds malformed or [0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal.checkPath` is invoked [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `copyMismatchMvHook`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The failure is not in the fuzzer harness but in the library code that computes[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontaining `..[0m[35m/[0m[39m` or absolute prefixes are not fully neutralized by the existing [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Inside the loop, it replaces:  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Path resolved = [0m[1;35msafeBase.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mnextEntry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Directory creation and subsequent file operations remain under the new [0m        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Patch Result  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Applying the above changes shifts the sanitizer failure point down four lines [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mnow at `Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:518[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but does not prevent Jazzer from detecting a [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath-traversal when handling certain entries.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack trace still shows `FilePathTraversal.check` invoked by [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`copyMismatchMvHook`, indicating that another extraction branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., mismatch [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrename, symbolic-link handling, or recursive expand[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m allows a crafted entry to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbypass the newly added check.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Other Extraction Branches**: The patch covers the primary code path for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolving entries in the main loop, but there are multiple helper methods [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`copyMismatchMvHook`, stream-based extraction, symlink creation[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that also compute[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand write file paths.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Recursive `expand` Calls**: The method recurses for nested archives. Each [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrecursive call should apply the same safe-resolution logic. Inspect how nested [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`targetDirPath` and `safeBase` propagate.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mismatch/Mv Hook**: The sanitizer failure occurs inside the [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“copyMismatchMvHook”. Examine how this hook derives destination paths and whether [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit uses the same `safeBase` logic.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Symlink and Hardlink Handling**: Verify that link targets are sanitized and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot written outside the base directory.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Normalization of Entry Names**: Ensure `[0m[1;35mnextEntry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitized—for example, stripping drive letters, UNC paths, or URI schemes before [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolving.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m489[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:470[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m505[0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m481[0m[39m:                Path target = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m483[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m484[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mFiles.isSameFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlink.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, parent[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m486[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m487[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mFiles.isRegularFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlink[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && ![0m[1;35mFiles.isSymbolicLink[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlink[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m488[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mFiles.createSymbolicLink[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlink, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m489[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m490[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m! [0m[1;35mzae.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m491[0m[39m:                Path target = [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m492[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m493[0m[39m:                    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m-> '%s'"[0m[39m,[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m494[0m[39m:                            targetDirectory, [0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m495[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m496[0m[39m:                Path parent = [0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m497[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m! [0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m498[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mparent.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m499[0m[39m:                    target = [0m[1;35mparent.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m500[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m501[0m[39m:                try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35marchive.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mzae[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m502[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mFiles.copy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m503[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m504[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m505[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Centralize and strengthen path resolution:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Introduce a private helper `[0m[1;35msafeResolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath safeBase, String entryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Takes `safeBase = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Computes `resolved = [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35msafeBase.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Throws `[0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"File path traversal: …"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` if [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`![0m[1;35mresolved.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Returns `resolved`.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Replace *all* occurrences of `[0m[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and manual [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`resolve/normalize` logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mZIP regular-file branch and symlink branch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35msafeResolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase, entryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. This unifies path‐slip prevention for every [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive entry.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Harden parent-directory creation to guard symlink chains:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Modify `createParentDirectory` into `[0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectorySafe[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath safeBase,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPath target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Begin from `Path current = safeBase`.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Compute `relative = [0m[1;35msafeBase.relativize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - For each segment `p` in `relative`:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         i.   `current = [0m[1;35mcurrent.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ii.  If `[0m[1;35mFiles.isSymbolicLink[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcurrent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, resolve to its real path via [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`current = [0m[1;35mcurrent.toRealPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor readLink + resolve against parent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, then [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mre‐normalize.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         iii. After any symlink resolution or creation, ensure [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mcurrent.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. If not, throw `IOException`.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         iv.  If `![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcurrent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcurrent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Return `current`.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Use `[0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectorySafe[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase, targetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in both generic and ZIP[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpand flows instead of the old method.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch the generic expand loop:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - At the top of `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mArchiveEntrySupplier<T>, ArchiveEntryBiConsumer<T>, Path[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Compute `safeBase` once.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the loop, replace:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `Path targetPath = nullTarget ? null : [0m[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     with[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `Path targetPath = nullTarget ? null : [0m[1;35msafeResolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase, [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnextEntry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After obtaining `targetPath`, if it’s a directory, call [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`; if a file, call [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectorySafe[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase, targetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` then write the stream. This [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensures the same safety checks in the generic path.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Patch the ZIP-specific expand method:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - At method entry, compute `safeBase` similarly.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Symlink branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m477[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m489[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Replace `Path link = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` with[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `Path link = [0m[1;35msafeResolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase, [0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Validate `targetName` does not denote an absolute path or contain `[0m[32m".."[0m[39m`. If[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit does, throw `IOException`.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • For parent directory under `link`, call `[0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectorySafe[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlink[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Create the symlink via `[0m[1;35mFiles.createSymbolicLink[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlink, [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. Since `link` is safe, the sanitizer cannot complain.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Regular-file branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m491[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m503[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Replace the existing resolve/normalize/startsWith logic with:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `Path target = [0m[1;35msafeResolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase, [0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Parent dir via `[0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectorySafe[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Copy the stream into `target`.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Ensure recursion inherits the same `safeBase`:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any recursive `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls must compute their `safeBase` from the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*original* top-level `targetDirectory`. Do not derive a new base from a nested [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`targetPath`. This means each `expand` invocation recomputes `safeBase` from its [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mown `targetDirectory`, but since nested calls pass a subdir of the top-level, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontainment is automatically enforced.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Do *not* modify harness or fuzzing logic. All changes stay within [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Expander.java`.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRationale:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A unified `safeResolve` ensures every entry—ZIP files, symlinks, TAR streams, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnested archives—undergoes the same absolute‐normalize‐startsWith guard.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Strengthening `createParentDirectory` to enforce `safeBase` containment at every [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath segment prevents symlink chains from escaping the target.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This approach preserves existing functionality [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdirectories, files, symlinks, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnested archives[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m while closing all discovered path-traversal holes that reached [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJazzer’s `copyMismatchMvHook`.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Potential side-effects: Tests that deliberately rely on creating symlink targets [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutside the base will now fail. However, path-traversal exploits are disallowed by [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdesign; legitimate tooling should not require escaping the extraction root.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Similar pattern already exists in Apache Commons for anti-“zip-slip” checks; here[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwe generalize and apply across all branches in `Expander`.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“safe base” path [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`safeBase`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and replaces all plain `resolve`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`normalize` calls [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m521[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m522[0m[39m:        return current;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m523[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   We will reapply and correctly integrate the “safeResolve” and [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“createParentDirectorySafe” helpers into `Expander.java`, then update both `expand`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethods [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe `ZipFile`-based overload and the generic `ArchiveStreamSupplier` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverload[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to use these helpers for all entry resolutions and parent-directory [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreations. This ensures no path [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding via symlinks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m can escape the intended [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutput directory, and it restores proper brace matching and compilation.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Detailed Steps  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Insert helper methods at class scope  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Locate the existing `private static Path [0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath root, Path[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m508[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and its closing brace.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Immediately after that closing brace—and before the next helper [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`prefersSeekableByteChannel`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m—insert two new private static methods:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35msafeResolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath safeBase, String entryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Resolves `entryName` against `safeBase`, normalizes, and throws [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException` if the result lies outside `safeBase`.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectorySafe[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath safeBase, Path target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Walks each segment of `[0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, follows symlinks safely [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mre-resolving them within `safeBase`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, enforces all intermediate paths stay under [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`safeBase`, and creates any missing directories.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Update ZipFile-based `expand` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m470[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m505[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After ensuring `targetDirectory` exists, define:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `final Path safeBase = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace all uses of `[0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand the manual [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`normalize`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`startsWith` checks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `Path link = [0m[1;35msafeResolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase, [0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `…`  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `Path target = [0m[1;35msafeResolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase, [0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfor regular files[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace calls to the old `[0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `Path parent = [0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectorySafe[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase, link[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `…`  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `[0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectorySafe[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase, target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` before copying.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Validate symlink targets by rejecting any `targetName` that is absolute or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontains `..`, to avoid creating symlinks outside the safe base.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Update generic-stream `expand` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mArchiveStreamSupplier[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Immediately after:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `final Path targetDirPath = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     add:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `final Path safeBase = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `[0m[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     with:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `[0m[1;35msafeResolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase, [0m[1;35mnextEntry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Where directories are created or parent directories are ensured, switch from [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `[0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectorySafe[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeBase, targetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   D. Imports  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure `java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets` and `java.io.IOException` are [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimported [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthey already are in `Expander.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   E. Brace matching & placement  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify that the helper methods are placed at the same indentation level as [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting private methods, and that no extraneous `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` or `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` were introduced.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm there remains exactly one closing brace at the end of the class.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach preserves all existing functionality: archives still expand, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msymlinks are still created when appropriate, and directory hierarchy is honored.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By applying checks centrally in `safeResolve` and `createParentDirectorySafe`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwe prevent both simple “zip slip” via `[0m[1;35mresolve[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` escapes and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msymlink-based traversals.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We avoid modifying any external libraries, test harnesses, or fuzzing [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic—only `Expander.java` is touched.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Placing the new methods after the original `createParentDirectory` retains [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbackward compatibility and avoids disturbing unrelated helper methods.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Proper brace placement eliminates the compilation errors [0m[1;39m([0m[39m“class, interface, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor enum expected”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m by ensuring methods are declared at the class level.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing code that relied on following symlinks outside the archive root will [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnow be rejected. However, such behavior was insecure [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCVE-style[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and is unlikely to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe required by consumers of the example code.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any tests expecting the old `createParentDirectory` helper to handle symlinks [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsafely will now fail; in that rare case we can preserve the old helper unmodified[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39munused[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for other formats and rely on the new safe version only in `expand`.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Performance impact is minimal—checking `startsWith` and a small loop per [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Reference Code Ranges  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Original ZipFile-based expand: `Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:470[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m505[0m[39m`  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Original createParentDirectory: `Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:508[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m523[0m[39m`  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith these changes, the class will compile cleanly, maintain full [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchival-expansion functionality, and close the security hole.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
